</p><p>The second single "<a href="/wiki/Perfume_(Britney_Spears_song)" title="Perfume (Britney Spears song)">Perfume</a>" premiered on November 3, 2013, two days earlier than originally announced.<sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup> It debuted and peaked at number 76 on the U.S. <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Hot_100" title="Billboard Hot 100"><i>Billboard</i> Hot 100</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup> In October 2013, she was featured as a guest vocalist on <a href="/wiki/Miley_Cyrus" title="Miley Cyrus">Miley Cyrus</a>'s track "<a href="/wiki/SMS_(Bangerz)" title="SMS (Bangerz)">SMS (Bangerz)</a>", taken from her fourth studio album <i><a href="/wiki/Bangerz" title="Bangerz">Bangerz</a></i> (2013).<sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup> On January 8, 2014, Spears won Favorite Pop Artist at the <a href="/wiki/40th_People%27s_Choice_Awards" title="40th People&#39;s Choice Awards">40th People's Choice Awards</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Microsoft_Theater" title="Microsoft Theater">Microsoft Theater</a> in Los Angeles.<sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup> In August 2014, Spears confirmed she had renewed her contract with RCA and that she was writing and recording new music for her next album.<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup> Spears announced through her Twitter account in August 2014 that she would be releasing an intimate apparel line called "The Intimate Britney Spears". It was available to be purchased beginning on September 9, 2014 in the United States and Canada through Spears's Intimate Collection website. It was later available on September 25 for purchase in Europe. The company now ships to over 200 countries including Australia and New Zealand.<sup id="cite_ref-190" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup> On September 25, 2014, Spears confirmed on <i><a href="/wiki/Good_Morning_Britain_(2014_TV_programme)" title="Good Morning Britain (2014 TV programme)">Good Morning Britain</a></i> that she had extended her contract with The AXIS and Planet Hollywood Resort &amp; Casino, to continue Britney: Piece of Me for two additional years.<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In March 2015, it was confirmed by <a href="/wiki/People_(magazine)" title="People (magazine)"><i>People</i> magazine</a> that Spears would release a new single, "<a href="/wiki/Pretty_Girls_(Britney_Spears_and_Iggy_Azalea_song)" title="Pretty Girls (Britney Spears and Iggy Azalea song)">Pretty Girls</a>", with <a href="/wiki/Iggy_Azalea" title="Iggy Azalea">Iggy Azalea</a>, on May 4, 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-192" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> The song debuted and peaked at number 29 on the <i>Billboard</i> Hot 100 and charted moderately in international territories. Spears and Azalea performed the track live at the <a href="/wiki/2015_Billboard_Music_Awards" title="2015 Billboard Music Awards">2015 Billboard Music Awards</a> from The AXIS, the home of Spears's residency, to positive critical response. <i>Entertainment Weekly</i> praised the performance, noting "Spears gave one of her most energetic televised performances in years."<sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup> On June 16, 2015, <a href="/wiki/Giorgio_Moroder" title="Giorgio Moroder">Giorgio Moroder</a> released his album, <i><a href="/wiki/D%C3%A9j%C3%A0_Vu_(Giorgio_Moroder_album)" title="D√©j√† Vu (Giorgio Moroder album)">Deja Vu</a></i>, that featured Spears on "<a href="/wiki/Tom%27s_Diner#Giorgio_Moroder_version" title="Tom&#39;s Diner">Tom's Diner</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup> The song was released as the fourth single from the album on October 9.<sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup> In an interview, Moroder praised Spears's vocals and said that she did a "good job" with the song and also stated that Spears "sounds so good that you would hardly recognize her."<sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup> At the <a href="/wiki/2015_Teen_Choice_Awards" title="2015 Teen Choice Awards">2015 Teen Choice Awards</a>, Spears received the Candie's Style Icon Award, her ninth Teen Choice Award.<sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup> In November, Spears guest starred as a fictionalized version of herself on <a href="/wiki/The_CW" title="The CW">The CW</a> series, <i><a href="/wiki/Jane_the_Virgin" title="Jane the Virgin">Jane the Virgin</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup> On the show, she danced to "Toxic" with <a href="/wiki/Gina_Rodriguez_(actress)" class="mw-redirect" title="Gina Rodriguez (actress)">Gina Rodriguez</a>'s character.<sup id="cite_ref-VultureJane_200-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-VultureJane-200">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2016.E2.80.932017:_Glory_and_continued_residency"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016‚Äì2017:_Glory_and_continued_residency">2016‚Äì2017: <i>Glory</i> and continued residency</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Britney_Spears,_Roundhouse,_London_(Apple_Music_Festival_2016)_(30072929931)_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Britney_Spears%2C_Roundhouse%2C_London_%28Apple_Music_Festival_2016%29_%2830072929931%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-Britney_Spears%2C_Roundhouse%2C_London_%28Apple_Music_Festival_2016%29_%2830072929931%29_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="231" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Britney_Spears%2C_Roundhouse%2C_London_%28Apple_Music_Festival_2016%29_%2830072929931%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-Britney_Spears%2C_Roundhouse%2C_London_%28Apple_Music_Festival_2016%29_%2830072929931%29_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Britney_Spears%2C_Roundhouse%2C_London_%28Apple_Music_Festival_2016%29_%2830072929931%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-Britney_Spears%2C_Roundhouse%2C_London_%28Apple_Music_Festival_2016%29_%2830072929931%29_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2184" data-file-height="2968" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Britney_Spears,_Roundhouse,_London_(Apple_Music_Festival_2016)_(30072929931)_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Spears performing during the <a href="/wiki/Apple_Music_Festival" title="Apple Music Festival">Apple Music Festival</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Roundhouse_(venue)" title="Roundhouse (venue)">Roundhouse</a>, <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a> on September 27, 2016</div></div></div>
<p>In 2016, Spears confirmed via social media that she had begun recording her ninth studio album.<sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup> On March 1, 2016, <i><a href="/wiki/V_(American_magazine)" title="V (American magazine)">V</a></i> magazine announced that Spears would appear on the cover of its 100th issue, dated March 8, 2016, in addition to revealing three different covers shot by photographer <a href="/wiki/Mario_Testino" title="Mario Testino">Mario Testino</a> for the milestone publication.<sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup> Editor-in-chief of the magazine, Stephen Gan, revealed that Spears was selected for the "V100" issue because of her status as an icon in the industry. On the decision, Gan stated, "who in our world did not grow up listening to her music?"<sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup> In May 2016, Spears launched a <a href="/wiki/Casual_game" title="Casual game">casual</a> <a href="/wiki/Role-playing_video_game" title="Role-playing video game">role-play</a> gaming application titled <i>Britney Spears: American Dream</i>. The app, created by <a href="/wiki/Glu_Mobile" title="Glu Mobile">Glu Mobile</a>, was made available through both <a href="/wiki/IOS" title="IOS">iOS</a> and <a href="/wiki/Google_Play" title="Google Play">Google Play</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-billboard.com_204-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-billboard.com-204">&#91;204&#93;</a></sup> On May 22, 2016, Spears performed a medley of her past singles at the <a href="/wiki/2016_Billboard_Music_Awards" title="2016 Billboard Music Awards">2016 Billboard Music Awards</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">&#91;205&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-206" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-206">&#91;206&#93;</a></sup> In addition to opening the show, Spears was honored with the <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Millennium_Award" class="mw-redirect" title="Billboard Millennium Award">Billboard Millennium Award</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">&#91;207&#93;</a></sup> On July 14, 2016, Spears released the lead single, "<a href="/wiki/Make_Me..._(Britney_Spears_song)" title="Make Me... (Britney Spears song)">Make Me...</a>", from her ninth studio album, featuring guest vocals from American rapper <a href="/wiki/G-Eazy" title="G-Eazy">G-Eazy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-208" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-208">&#91;208&#93;</a></sup> The album, <i><a href="/wiki/Glory_(Britney_Spears_album)" title="Glory (Britney Spears album)">Glory</a></i>, was formally released on August 26, 2016. On August 16, 2016, <a href="/wiki/MTV" title="MTV">MTV</a> and Spears announced that she would perform at the <a href="/wiki/2016_MTV_Video_Music_Awards" title="2016 MTV Video Music Awards">2016 MTV Video Music Awards</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">&#91;209&#93;</a></sup> The performance marked Spears's first time returning to the VMA stage after her widely controversial performance of "Gimme More" at the 2007 show nine years earlier.<sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">&#91;210&#93;</a></sup> Along with "Make Me...", Spears and G-Eazy also performed the latter's hit song "<a href="/wiki/Me,_Myself_%26_I_(G-Eazy_and_Bebe_Rexha_song)" title="Me, Myself &amp; I (G-Eazy and Bebe Rexha song)">Me, Myself &amp; I</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-211" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-211">&#91;211&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Spears appeared on the cover of <i><a href="/wiki/Marie_Claire" title="Marie Claire">Marie Claire</a></i> UK for the October 2016 issue. In the publication, Spears revealed that she had suffered from crippling anxiety in the past, and that motherhood played a major role in helping her overcome it.<sup id="cite_ref-212" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-212">&#91;212&#93;</a></sup> "My boys don't care if everything isn't perfect. They don't judge me," Spears said in the issue.<sup id="cite_ref-ETCanadaMC_213-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ETCanadaMC-213">&#91;213&#93;</a></sup> In November 2016, during an interview with Las Vegas Blog, Spears confirmed she had already begun work on her next album, stating: "I'm not sure what I want the next album to sound like. [...] I just know that I'm excited to get into the studio again and actually have already been back recording."<sup id="cite_ref-214" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-214">&#91;214&#93;</a></sup> In January 2017, Spears received four wins out of four nominations at the <a href="/wiki/43rd_People%27s_Choice_Awards" title="43rd People&#39;s Choice Awards">43rd People's Choice Awards</a>, including Favorite Pop Artist, Female Artist, Social Media celebrity as well as Comedic Collaboration for a skit with <a href="/wiki/Ellen_DeGeneres" title="Ellen DeGeneres">Ellen DeGeneres</a> for <i><a href="/wiki/The_Ellen_DeGeneres_Show" title="The Ellen DeGeneres Show">The Ellen DeGeneres Show</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-215" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-215">&#91;215&#93;</a></sup> In March 2017, Spears announced that her residency concert would be performed abroad as a world tour, <a href="/wiki/Britney:_Live_in_Concert" title="Britney: Live in Concert">Britney: Live in Concert</a>, with dates in select Asian cities.<sup id="cite_ref-216" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-216">&#91;216&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-217" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-217">&#91;217&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-218" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-218">&#91;218&#93;</a></sup> In April 2017, the <a href="/wiki/Israeli_Labor_Party" title="Israeli Labor Party">Israeli Labor Party</a> announced that it would reschedule its July primary election to avoid conflict with Spears's sold-out Tel Aviv concert, citing traffic and security concerns.<sup id="cite_ref-219" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-219">&#91;219&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Spears's manager Larry Rudolph also announced the residency would not be extended following her contract expiration with Caesars Entertainment at the end of 2017. On April 29, 2017, Spears became the first recipient of the Icon Award at the <a href="/wiki/2017_Radio_Disney_Music_Awards" title="2017 Radio Disney Music Awards">2017 Radio Disney Music Awards</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-220" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-220">&#91;220&#93;</a></sup> On November 4, 2017, Spears attended the grand opening of the Nevada Childhood Cancer Foundation Britney Spears Campus in <a href="/wiki/Las_Vegas" title="Las Vegas">Las Vegas</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-221" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-221">&#91;221&#93;</a></sup> Later that month, <i><a href="/wiki/Forbes" title="Forbes">Forbes</a></i> announced that Spears was the 8th highest earning female musician, earning $34&#160;million in 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-222" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-222">&#91;222&#93;</a></sup> On December 31, 2017, Spears performed the final show of Britney: Piece of Me.<sup id="cite_ref-iheart.com_223-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-iheart.com-223">&#91;223&#93;</a></sup> The final performance reportedly brought in $1.172&#160;million, setting a new box office record for a single show in Las Vegas, and breaking the record previously held by <a href="/wiki/Jennifer_Lopez" title="Jennifer Lopez">Jennifer Lopez</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-iheart.com_223-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-iheart.com-223">&#91;223&#93;</a></sup> The last show was broadcast live with performances of "<a href="/wiki/Toxic_(song)" title="Toxic (song)">Toxic</a>" and "<a href="/wiki/Work_Bitch" title="Work Bitch">Work Bitch</a>" airing on ABC's <i><a href="/wiki/Dick_Clark%27s_New_Year%27s_Rockin%27_Eve" title="Dick Clark&#39;s New Year&#39;s Rockin&#39; Eve">Dick Clark's New Year's Rockin' Eve</a></i> to a record audience of 25.6&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-224" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-224">&#91;224&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2018.E2.80.93present:_Piece_of_Me_Tour.2C_hiatus.2C_and_the_.23FreeBritney_movement"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018‚Äìpresent:_Piece_of_Me_Tour,_hiatus,_and_the_#FreeBritney_movement">2018‚Äìpresent: Piece of Me Tour, hiatus, and the #FreeBritney movement</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:162px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Britney_Spears_Domination.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Britney_Spears_Domination.jpg/160px-Britney_Spears_Domination.jpg" decoding="async" width="160" height="268" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Britney_Spears_Domination.jpg/240px-Britney_Spears_Domination.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/65/Britney_Spears_Domination.jpg 2x" data-file-width="266" data-file-height="446" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Britney_Spears_Domination.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Spears announcing her Domination concert residency in December 2018.</div></div></div>
<p>In January 2018, Spears released her 24th perfume with Elizabeth Arden, <a href="/wiki/Fantasy_(fragrance)#Sunset_Fantasy" title="Fantasy (fragrance)">Sunset Fantasy</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-225" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-225">&#91;225&#93;</a></sup> and announced the <a href="/wiki/Piece_of_Me_Tour" title="Piece of Me Tour">Piece of Me Tour</a> which took place in July 2018 in North American and Europe.<sup id="cite_ref-226" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-226">&#91;226&#93;</a></sup> Tickets were sold out within minutes for major cities, and additional dates were added to meet the demand.<sup id="cite_ref-227" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-227">&#91;227&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Pitbull_(rapper)" title="Pitbull (rapper)">Pitbull</a> was the <a href="/wiki/Supporting_act" class="mw-redirect" title="Supporting act">supporting act</a>  for the European leg.<sup id="cite_ref-228" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-228">&#91;228&#93;</a></sup> The tour ranked at 86 and 30 on Pollstar's 2018 Year-End Top 100 Tours chart both in North America and worldwide, respectively. In total, the tour grossed $54.3 million with 260,531 tickets sold and was the sixth highest-grossing female tour of 2018, and was the United Kingdom's second best-selling female tour of 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-229" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-229">&#91;229&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-230" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-230">&#91;230&#93;</a></sup> On March 20, 2018, Spears was announced as part of a campaign for French luxury fashion house <a href="/wiki/Kenzo_(brand)" title="Kenzo (brand)">Kenzo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-harpersbazaar.com.au_231-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-harpersbazaar.com.au-231">&#91;231&#93;</a></sup> The company said it aimed to shake up the 'jungle' world of fashion with Spears's 'La Collection Memento No. 2' campaign.<sup id="cite_ref-lvmh.com_232-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-lvmh.com-232">&#91;232&#93;</a></sup> On April 12, 2018, Spears was honored with the 2018 <a href="/wiki/GLAAD_Vanguard_Award" title="GLAAD Vanguard Award">GLAAD Vanguard Award</a> at the <a href="/wiki/GLAAD_Media_Award" title="GLAAD Media Award">GLAAD Media Awards</a> for her role in "accelerating acceptance for the LGBTQ community".<sup id="cite_ref-spearsglaad_233-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-spearsglaad-233">&#91;233&#93;</a></sup> On April 27, 2018, Epic Rights announced a new partnership with Spears to debut her own fashion line in 2019, which would include clothing, fitness apparel, accessories, and electronics.<sup id="cite_ref-234" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-234">&#91;234&#93;</a></sup> In July 2018, Spears released her first unisex fragrance, <a href="/wiki/Britney_Spears_products#Perfumes" title="Britney Spears products">Prerogative</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-235" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-235">&#91;235&#93;</a></sup> On October 21, 2018, Spears performed at the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Grand_Prix" title="United States Grand Prix">Formula One Grand Prix</a> in <a href="/wiki/Austin,_Texas" title="Austin, Texas">Austin</a>, which ultimately served as the final performance of her Piece of Me Tour.<sup id="cite_ref-236" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-236">&#91;236&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On October 18, 2018, Spears announced her second Las Vegas residency show, <a href="/wiki/Britney:_Domination" title="Britney: Domination">Britney: Domination</a>, which was set to launch at <a href="/wiki/Park_MGM" title="Park MGM">Park MGM</a>'s Park Theatre on February 13, 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-237" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-237">&#91;237&#93;</a></sup> Spears was slated to make $507,000 per show, which would have made her the highest paid act on the <a href="/wiki/Las_Vegas_Strip" title="Las Vegas Strip">Las Vegas Strip</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-238" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-238">&#91;238&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-239" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-239">&#91;239&#93;</a></sup> However, on January 4, 2019, she announced that the residency was cancelled after her father had a near-fatal colon rupture. Her team also announced that Spears would go on an indefinite work hiatus, putting all activities and commitments on hold, so that she can spend time with her family.<sup id="cite_ref-hiatus_240-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hiatus-240">&#91;240&#93;</a></sup> In March 2019, Spears's co-conservator Andrew Wallet resigned, and said "Substantial detriment, irreparable harm and immediate danger will result to the conservatee and her estate if the relief requested herein in not granted on an ex parte basis."<sup id="cite_ref-241" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-241">&#91;241&#93;</a></sup> The same month, Spears reportedly entered a psychiatric facility to focus on <a href="/wiki/Self-care" title="Self-care">self-care</a> amidst stress from her father's illness.<sup id="cite_ref-billboardtakingmetime_242-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-billboardtakingmetime-242">&#91;242&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Podcast" title="Podcast">podcast</a> <i>Britney's Gram</i> alleged, according to information from an anonymous paralegal source, that Spears had been held against her will in the facility since January 2019. They claimed the hospitalization and <i>Domination</i> cancellation were ordered by Spears's father after she decided to not take her medication and violated rules in her conservatorship, specifically driving. <i>Britney's Gram</i> and several news outlets questioned the length of the conservatorship, as it was supposed to end after The Circus Tour in 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-243" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-243">&#91;243&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following the podcast, there was social media backlash to the alleged abuse of power and violation of human rights Spears has endured under a conservatorship by her father and the mismanagement of Lou Taylor, who was responsible for initiating the conservatorship.<sup id="cite_ref-244" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-244">&#91;244&#93;</a></sup> <i>TMZ</i> later posted several conflicting stories, detailing in a video that although Spears had not been formally diagnosed with <a href="/wiki/Bipolar_disorder" title="Bipolar disorder">bipolar disorder</a>, she is receiving medication for it, and justified this, which was later deleted.<sup id="cite_ref-245" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-245">&#91;245&#93;</a></sup> On April 22, 2019, fans held a protest outside the <a href="/wiki/West_Hollywood_City_Hall" title="West Hollywood City Hall">West Hollywood City Hall</a>, drawing attention towards the prolonged conservatorship, suggesting she was being detained against her will.<sup id="cite_ref-varietyfansdemand_246-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-varietyfansdemand-246">&#91;246&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-billboardfanshold_247-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-billboardfanshold-247">&#91;247&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-whatisactually_248-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-whatisactually-248">&#91;248&#93;</a></sup> Spears posted a video Instagram account  on April 24, assuring fans all is well and also addressed leaked emails about Lou Taylor, claiming they were written by her ex-manager Sam Lutfi."<sup id="cite_ref-bbcnewstellsfans_249-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcnewstellsfans-249">&#91;249&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-250" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-250">&#91;250&#93;</a></sup> Spears left the facility the following day.<sup id="cite_ref-etreleasedfrom_251-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-etreleasedfrom-251">&#91;251&#93;</a></sup> It was reported on April 24, 2019, that Spears would have a new conservatorship hearing for May 10, 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-252" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-252">&#91;252&#93;</a></sup> Spears attended the hearing with her mother.<sup id="cite_ref-bsappears_253-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bsappears-253">&#91;253&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-thebattle_254-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-thebattle-254">&#91;254&#93;</a></sup> Following the hearing, an investigation was ordered into Spears's conservatorship.<sup id="cite_ref-microscope_255-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-microscope-255">&#91;255&#93;</a></sup> According to alleged reports by <i>TMZ</i>, she stated in court that she was forcibly put into the mental health facility.<sup id="cite_ref-forced_256-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-forced-256">&#91;256&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-postbattle_257-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-postbattle-257">&#91;257&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On September 3, 2019, it was reported that Spears' father and conservator allegedly abused her thirteen year old son, Sean Preston. Law enforcement spoke to <i>The Blast</i> to report the incident, stating Kevin Federline filed a police report on August 25.<sup id="cite_ref-258" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-258">&#91;258&#93;</a></sup> It was later reported that Jamie Spears was reportedly so enraged during an argument with his 13-year-old grandson that he broke down a door to get to the young boy, and the incident has sparked a child abuse investigation. Britney then sent her sons back to their father's home, despite it still being her custodial visit time.<sup id="cite_ref-259" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-259">&#91;259&#93;</a></sup> Spears' two sons have since been granted a three year restraining order against their grandfather.<sup id="cite_ref-260" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-260">&#91;260&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Artistry">Artistry</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Influences">Influences</span></h3>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r889293853/mw-parser-output/.tmulti">.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbinner{display:flex;flex-direction:column}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .trow{display:flex;flex-direction:row;clear:left;flex-wrap:wrap;width:100%;box-sizing:border-box}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .tsingle{margin:1px;float:left}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .theader{clear:both;font-weight:bold;text-align:center;align-self:center;background-color:transparent;width:100%}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbcaption{text-align:left;background-color:transparent}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .text-align-left{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .text-align-right{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .text-align-center{text-align:center}@media all and (max-width:720px){.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbinner{width:100%!important;box-sizing:border-box;max-width:none!important;align-items:center}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .trow{justify-content:center}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .tsingle{float:none!important;max-width:100%!important;box-sizing:border-box;text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbcaption{text-align:center}}</style><div class="thumb tmulti tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:274px;max-width:274px"><div class="trow"><div class="tsingle" style="width:135px;max-width:135px"><div class="thumbimage"><a
